\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mqtt\+Test\+Task()}{mqttTestTask()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily void mqtt\+Test\+Task (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{void $\ast$}]{param }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



The main block of the Program. Calls all the relevant sections at the correct time. 

Configure gateway communication channels

Establish Node Communication Channels

Begin Node Communication

Communicates immediately when a Node fails. Stopped a critical bug.

Sends all the valid and working node\textquotesingle{}s data to the cloud.

\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{client\+Cert}{clientCert}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \hyperlink{compiler__port_8h_a40bb5262bf908c328fbcfbe5d29d0201}{char\+\_\+t} client\+Cert\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}

{\bfseries Initial value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
=
        \textcolor{stringliteral}{"-----BEGIN CERTIFICATE-----"}
        \textcolor{stringliteral}{"-----END CERTIFICATE-----"}
\end{DoxyCode}
This is the x509 certificate provided by the M\+Q\+TT service. Each line of the cert should be delimited by double quotes(\char`\"{}\char`\"{}), including the Begin and End Certificate lines.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \hyperlink{compiler__port_8h_a40bb5262bf908c328fbcfbe5d29d0201}{char\+\_\+t} client\+Key\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}

{\bfseries Initial value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
=
        \textcolor{stringliteral}{"-----BEGIN RSA PRIVATE KEY-----"}
        \textcolor{stringliteral}{"-----END RSA PRIVATE KEY-----"}
\end{DoxyCode}
This is the private key provided by the M\+Q\+TT service. Each line of the cert should be delimited by double quotes(\char`\"{}\char`\"{}), including the Begin and End Certificate lines.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily const \hyperlink{compiler__port_8h_a40bb5262bf908c328fbcfbe5d29d0201}{char\+\_\+t} trusted\+Ca\+List\mbox{[}$\,$\mbox{]}}
